  <script>

  (function(){

    // banner settings

    let atOpenNewTab = true; /* true or false */



    // banner image values

    var atImageURL = "https://www.marriott.com/marriottassets/search/homepage/Joe/MBV_app3_748x332.png";

    let atImgAltCopy = 'Marriott Bonvoy App';



    // banner copy

    let atHeaderCopy = "It's all right here with the Marriott Bonvoy App";

    let atBodyCopy = '';

    let atCTACopy = 'Learn More';

    let atCTAurl = 'https://marriott.app.link/tdEAPp3Hy4';



    // impression & click tracking values

    let trackingContentPosition = 'allOtherPagesFooterBanner';

    let trackingOfferType = 'app'; /* booking, loyalty, cobrand, hvmi, app */

    let trackingDescription = 'unlockYourStay1120';

    let trackingTag = 'US-';



    let atCTAclickTrackVal = 'Banner|' + trackingDescription + '|external|event167,list3=' + trackingContentPosition + ';type=' + trackingOfferType + ';msg=' + trackingDescription + ';tag=' + trackingTag;



    function getCookie(cname) {

      var name = cname + "=";

      var ca = document.cookie.split(';');

      for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

        var c = ca[i];

        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {

          c = c.substring(1);

        }

        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

          return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

        }

      }

      return "";

    }



    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes) {

      var d = new Date();

      d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);

      var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

      document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";

    }



    function atBannerUpdate() {

      // updates banner template update

      let atBannerTemplate = '<section class="atAdBannerBannerContainer mi-sub-section sub-section l-bleed-on-mobile"><div class="l-display-flex l-display-flex-wrap l-print-fullbleed l-container"><div class="atAdBannerBanner"><div class="atAdBannerBannerImg"><picture><source media="(min-width: 601px)" srcset="' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* , ' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* 2x " ></source> <source media="(max-width: 600px)" srcset="' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* , ' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* 2x" ></source> <img alt="' + atImgAltCopy + '" src="' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* , ' + atImageURL + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=480px:* 2x " /></picture></div><div class="atAdBannerBannerRightContainer"><div class="atAdBannerBannerCopy"><div class="atAdBannerBannerCopyHeadline">' + atHeaderCopy + '</div></div><div class="atAdBannerBannerCTA"><a class="m-button m-button-secondary mi-popover custom_click_track" custom_click_track_value="' + atCTAclickTrackVal + '" href="' + atCTAurl + '" target=""><span class="mtCC-cta-span">' + atCTACopy + '</span></a></div></div></div></div> </section>';

      var refNode = document.querySelector('#main-body-wrapper > footer');

      refNode.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", atBannerTemplate);



      // Open in a new tab or not icon

      if (atOpenNewTab == true) {

        document.querySelector('section.atAdBannerBannerContainer .atAdBannerBannerCTA a').setAttribute('target', '_blank');

        document.querySelector('section.atAdBannerBannerContainer .atAdBannerBannerCTA a').innerHTML = '<span class="mtCC-cta-span">' + atCTACopy + '</span><span aria-label="Opens in a new browser window." class="t-icon-external-site"> </span>';

      }           

    }



    var atCallback = function () {

      // merchandising impression tracking

      let cname = "merchViewed";

      let cvalue = trackingContentPosition + "-" + trackingDescription;

      let minutes = 30;

      let ctemp = getCookie(cname) || "";

      if (ctemp.includes(cvalue) !== true) {

        if (typeof atCArray !== "object") {

          atCArray = [];

        };

        atCArray.push(cvalue);

      };

      if (typeof atMArray !== "object") {

        atMArray = [];

      };

      atMArray.push(trackingContentPosition + ',type=' + trackingOfferType + ',msg=' + trackingDescription + ',tag=' + trackingTag);

      //impressionTrack('event168|list3=' + trackingContentPosition + ',type=' + trackingOfferType + ',msg=' + trackingDescription + ',tag=' + trackingTag);

      atBannerUpdate();  

    };



    if ( document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {

      atCallback();      

    } else {

      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", atCallback);

    }

  })();

</script>

          newContent = '<section class="tile-card-article l-template-1 l-left-align l-s-col-4 l-m-col-8 l-l-col-12 l-xl-col-12 l-display-inline-block "> <div class="img-wrapper l-s-col-4 l-l-col-12"> <picture> <source srcset="' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=1180px:* , ' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&downsize=2360px:* 2x" media="(min-width: 1025px)"> <source srcset="' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=1024px:*, ' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&downsize=2048px:* 2x" media="(min-width: 769px)"> <source srcset="' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=768px:*" media="(min-width: 601px)"> <source srcset="' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=600px:*"> <img src="' + imageURL + '?output-quality=70&interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=600px:*" data-altflag="false" alt="' + altCopy + '"> </picture> </div><div class="title-desc-cta l-padding-none l-display-inline-block"> <div class="title-desc "> <div class="l-s-margin-bottom-none l-l-margin-bottom"> <ul> <li>' + bullet1 + '</li><li>' + bullet2 + '</li><li>'  +  bullet3 + '</li></ul> </div></div><div class="cta l-s-col-4 l-s-margin-bottom l-pos-relative "> <a class="m-button m-button-secondary-fill-alt l-width-max l-padding-top l-padding-bottom mi-popover analytics-click custom_click_track" custom_click_track_value="' + clickTrackValue + '" href="' + ctaURL + '">' + ctaCopy + '</a> </div></div></section>';

  

      function getCookie(cname) {

          var name = cname + "=";

          var ca = document.cookie.split(';');

          for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

              var c = ca[i];

              while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {

                  c = c.substring(1);

              }

              if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

                  return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

              }

          }

          return "";

      }

  

      function setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes) {

          var d = new Date();

          d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);

          var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

          document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";

      }

  

      function waitFor(selector, callback) {

          let error = true,

              tryAgain = 100,

              element,

              timer = setInterval(function() {

                  element = document.querySelector(selector)

                  if (element) {

                      callback(element);

                      error = false;

                      tryAgain = 0;

                  }

                  if (--tryAgain < 1) {

                      if (error) {

                          console.log('element was not found');

                      }

                      clearInterval(timer);

                  }

              },100);

      }

  

      function fireTracking() {

          // merchandising impression tracking

          let cname = "merchViewed";

          let cvalue = trackingPosition + "-" + trackingDescription;

          let minutes = 30;

          let ctemp = getCookie(cname) || "";

  

          if (ctemp.includes(cvalue) !== true) {

              cvalue = ctemp + cvalue + "|";

              setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes);

          };

  

          impressionTrack('event168|list3=' + trackingPosition + ',type=' + trackingOfferType + ',msg=' + trackingDescription + ',tag=' + trackingTag);

      }

      

      function updateContent() {

          // check for AEM selector then ARIES selector for remembered and unauthenticated states AND if exists add click event to update content and fire tracking

          var clickTarget;

          if (dataLayer.env_platform.includes('AEM')) {

              clickTarget = document.querySelector('a[data-overlay-endpoint="/signInOverlay.mi"]');

          } else if (dataLayer.env_platform.includes('ram') && dataLayer.mr_prof_authentication_state == 'remembered') {

              clickTarget = document.querySelector('a[href="/signInOverlay.mi"]');

          } else if (dataLayer.env_platform.includes('ram') && dataLayer.mr_prof_authentication_state == 'unauthenticated') {

              clickTarget = document.querySelector('a[data-modal-target="/signInOverlay.mi"]');

          }

          if (clickTarget !== null && clickTarget !== undefined) {

              clickTarget.addEventListener('click', function() {

                  waitFor('div.modal-content section.two-col-sub-section > div:nth-child(2) h3', function(target) {

                      target.innerHTML = headerCopy;

                  });

                  waitFor('.modal-content [id^="CardArticle"]', function(target) {

                      target.innerHTML = newContent;

                  });

                  fireTracking();

              });

          }            

      }

  

      if ( document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {

          updateContent();

      } else {

          document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", updateContent);

      }

  })();

</script>

  <script class="at-element-marker">

  (function () {

    function getCookie(cname) {

      var name = cname + "=";

      var ca = document.cookie.split(";");

      for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {

        var c = ca[i];

        while (c.charAt(0) == " ") {

          c = c.substring(1);

        }

        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

          return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

        }

      }

      return "";

    }



    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes) {

      var d = new Date();

      d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);

      var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

      document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";

    }



    var atCallback = function () {

      if (typeof atMArray == "object") {

        var atMCampVal = atMArray.join('^');

        impressionTrack("event168|list3=" + atMCampVal);

      };



      if (typeof atCArray == "object") {

        let cname = "merchViewed";

        let cvalue = atCArray.join('|');

        let minutes = 30;

        let ctemp = getCookie(cname) || "";

        cvalue = ctemp + cvalue + "|";

        setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes);

      };

    };



    if ( document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {

      atCallback();

    } else {

      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", atCallback);

    }

  })();

/*LOAD A SCRIPT WITH A CALLBACK FUNCTION*/

function launchLoadScriptCallback(a, c, b) {

    var d = document.getElementsByTagName("script"),

        e;

    b = d[0];

    for (e = 0; e < d.length; e++)

        if (d[e].src === a && d[e].readyState && /loaded|complete/.test(d[e].readyState)) try {

            c()

        } catch (g) {} finally {

            return

        }

    d = document.createElement("script");

    d.type = "text/javascript";

    d.async = !0;

    d.src = a;

    d.onerror = function() {

        this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded")

    };

    d.onload = d.onreadystatechange = function() {

        if (!this.readyState ||

            "complete" === this.readyState || "loaded" === this.readyState) {

            this.onload = this.onreadystatechange = null;

            this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded");

            try {

                c.call(this)

            } catch (g) {}

        }

    };

    b.parentNode.insertBefore(d, b)

}



/*LOAD A SCRIPT WITH A CALLBACK FUNCTION*/

    b = d[0];

            c()

        } catch (g) {} finally {

            return

        }

    d = document.createElement("script");

    d.type = "text/javascript";

    d.async = false;

  console.log('Kasada value of d.async is : '+d.async);

    d.src = a;

    d.onerror = function() {

        this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded")

    };

            "complete" === this.readyState || "loaded" === this.readyState) {

            this.onload = this.onreadystatechange = null;

            this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded");

            try {

                c.call(this)

            } catch (g) {}

        }

    };

    b.parentNode.insertBefore(d, b)

}

function launchImage(a) {

    var c = new Image(0, 0);

    c.src = a;

    c.alt = "Tag";/*FOR ADR COMPLIANCE*/

    return c

}



/*INCLUDE A NEW SCRIPT*/

function launchScript(src, async) {

  //console.log('The src fired is : '+src);

    var newScript = document.createElement('script');

    newScript.type = 'text/javascript';

    newScript.src = src; //URL

    newScript.async = (typeof async !== "undefined")?async:true;

    document.head.appendChild(newScript);

}



/*INCLUDE A NEW IFRAME*/

function launchIframe(src) {

    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');

    iframe.style.display = "none";

    iframe.src = src;

    document.body.appendChild(iframe);

}



function getCookie(cname) {

  var name = cname + "=";

  var decodedCookie = decodeURI(document.cookie);

  var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');

  for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {

    var c = ca[i];

    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {

      c = c.substring(1);

    }

    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {

      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);

    }

  }

  return "";

}



/*IT fires this function when click actions happen for most elements but not all. It passes info specific to the element and action*/

window._trackAnalytics = function(obj) {

  if (typeof obj === "object") {

    if (typeof window.trackAnalyticsOjb === 'undefined') {

      window.trackAnalyticsObj = '';

    }

    window.trackAnalyticsObj = JSON.stringify(obj);

    //populate Tile Names in dataLayer

    if (typeof obj.tiles != "undefined") {

      var tempList = "";

      $.each(obj.tiles, function(index, value) {

        tempList += value.name;

        //check for errors, add loaded status

        if (typeof value.error !== "undefined") {

          tempList += "_Not Loaded|";

        } else {

          tempList += "_Loaded|";

        }

        //tempList += value.id.substring(0, value.id.lastIndexOf("_") ) + "|";

      });

      tempList = tempList.replace(/\|\s*$/, "");

      dataLayer.ram_tile_names = tempList;

      

    }

    if (typeof obj.page_data_layer_ready != "undefined" && obj.page_data_layer_ready == "true") {

      dataLayer.page_data_layer_ready = "true";

    }

    /*console log message only if debug is turned on*/

    _satellite.logger.log("_trackAnalytics call JSON: ", JSON.stringify(obj));

  }

};

/** Check for "interactionCount" value from OneTrust cookie OptanonConsent. Value of '0' means it is a new user **/

function getOneTrustInteractionCount(){

  let interactionCount = 1;

  let optCookie = _satellite.cookie.get("OptanonConsent");

  if(optCookie.indexOf('&interactionCount=0&')>-1){

    interactionCount = 0;

  }

  return interactionCount;

}



/** send opt-in/out status to analytics **/

function sendOptInStatusToAnalytics(){

  //1 is opted in so 6:1 is opted into analytics

  let analyticsOptedIn = true;//6:1

  let advertOptedIn = true;//4:1

  let optCookie = _satellite.cookie.get("OptanonConsent");

  if (optCookie != null && optCookie.indexOf('groups')>-1 ) {

      var obj = {};

      var x = decodeURIComponent(window.getCookie("OptanonConsent")).split("&");

      for (var i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {

          var split = x[i].split('=');

          obj[split[0].trim()] = split[1].trim();

      }

      console.log(obj.groups.indexOf("6:0"));

      if (obj.groups && obj.groups.indexOf("6:0") != -1) {

          analyticsOptedIn = false;

          console.log("analyticsOptedIn = false");

      } 

      if (obj.groups && obj.groups.indexOf("4:0") != -1) {

          advertOptedIn = false;

          console.log("analyticsOptedIn = false");

      } 

      let advertEvar = advertOptedIn ? "Opted In" : "Opted Out";

      let analyticsEvar = analyticsOptedIn ? "Opted In" : "Opted Out";

      _satellite.logger.log("OptanonConsent COOKIE EXISTS " +advertEvar+" "+analyticsEvar);

      let ccCode = _satellite.getVar("browser_akamai_loc_country");



      s.origLTV = s.linkTrackVars;

      s.origEvents = s.events;

      s.linkTrackVars = "eVar246,eVar248,eVar250,events";

      s.eVar246 = ccCode;

      s.eVar248 = advertEvar;

      s.eVar250 = analyticsEvar;

      s.linkTrackEvents = "event312";

      s.events = "event312"; 

      _satellite.logger.log("Firing s.tl call = "+ccCode+" "+advertEvar+" "+analyticsEvar);

      s.tl(this, "o", "Opt_In tracking");

      s.linkTrackEvents = "None";

      s.linkTrackVars = s.origLTV;

      s.events = s.origEvents;

      //_satellite.setVar('overideOptOut', 'false');

  }else{

    console.log("OPT-OUT Failed - sendAnalytics - no OptAnaonCookie");

  } 

}

        function bindObjLoad(selector, fn) {

            // Store the selector and callback to be monitored

            listeners.push({

                selector: selector,

                fn: fn

            });

            if (!observer) {

                // Watch for changes in the document

                observer = new MutationObserver(bindObjLoadCheck);

                observer.observe(doc.documentElement, {

                    childList: true,

                    subtree: true

                });

            }

            // bindObjLoadCheck if the element is currently in the DOM

            bindObjLoadCheck();

        }



        function bindOn(selector, type, target, action) {

            switch (type) {

                case 'click':

                case "keyup":

                case "mousedown":

                    bindOnClick(selector, type, target, action);

                    break;

                case 'method':

                    bindOnMethod(selector, type, target, action);

                    break;

            }

        }



        function bindOnClick(selector, type, target, action) {

            var someInput = document.querySelector(selector);

            someInput.addEventListener(type, function(evt) {

                handleClick(evt, target, action);

            });

        }



        function bindOnMethod(obj, actionType, func, args) {

            mart.log('obj : ' + typeof obj);

            mart.log('actionType : ' + actionType);

            mart.log('func : ' + typeof func);

            func.apply(obj, args);

        }



        function handleClick(event, target, action) {

            var someOutput = document.querySelector(target);

            switch (action[0]) {

                case 'style.cssText':

                    someOutput.style.cssText = action[1];

                    break;

                case 'style.setProperty':

                    someOutput.style.setProperty = action[1];

                    break;

                case 'style.background':

                    someOutput.style.background = action[1];

                    break;

                case 'innerHTML':

                    someOutput.innerHTML = action[1];

                    break;

                case 'textContent':

                    someOutput.textContent = action[1];

                    break;

                case 'addClass':

                    someOutput.classList.add(action[1]);

                    break;

                case 'removeClass':

                    someOutput.classList.remove(action[1]);

                    break;

                case 'function':

                    console.log("action1 is " + action[1]);

                    console.log("inside a function @@@@" + typeof action[1]);

                    //console.log(eval(action[1]));

                    eval(action[1]);

                    break;

            }

        }



        function bindObjLoadCheck() {

            // bindObjLoadCheck the DOM for elements matching a stored selector

            for (var i = 0, len = listeners.length, listener, elements; i < len; i++) {

                listener = listeners[i];

                // Query for elements matching the specified selector

                elements = doc.querySelectorAll(listener.selector);

                for (var j = 0, jLen = elements.length, element; j < jLen; j++) {

                    element = elements[j];

                    // Make sure the callback isn't invoked with the

                    // same element more than once

                    if (!element.bindObjLoad) {

                        element.bindObjLoad = true;

                        // Invoke the callback with the element

                        listener.fn.call(element, element);

                    }

                }

            }

        }

        if (!window.mart_loglevel) {

            window.mart_loglevel = 0;

        }

        function hashMd5(d) {

            result = M(V(Y(X(d), 8 * d.length)));

            return result.toLowerCase();

        }



        function M(d) {

            for (var _, m = "0123456789ABCDEF", f = "", r = 0; r < d.length; r++) _ = d.charCodeAt(r), f += m.charAt(_ >>> 4 & 15) + m.charAt(15 & _);

            return f;

        }



        function X(d) {

            for (var _ = Array(d.length >> 2), m = 0; m < _.length; m++) _[m] = 0;

            for (m = 0; m < 8 * d.length; m += 8) _[m >> 5] |= (255 & d.charCodeAt(m / 8)) << m % 32;

            return _;

        }



        function V(d) {

            for (var _ = "", m = 0; m < 32 * d.length; m += 8) _ += String.fromCharCode(d[m >> 5] >>> m % 32 & 255);

            return _;

        }



        function Y(d, _) {

            d[_ >> 5] |= 128 << _ % 32, d[14 + (_ + 64 >>> 9 << 4)] = _;

            for (var m = 1732584193, f = -271733879, r = -1732584194, i = 271733878, n = 0; n < d.length; n += 16) {

718787259), i, m, d[n + 9], 21, -343485551), m = safe_add(m, h), f = safe_add(f, t), r = safe_add(r, g), i = safe_add(i, e);

            }

            return Array(m, f, r, i);

        }



        function md5_cmn(d, _, m, f, r, i) {

            return safe_add(bit_rol(safe_add(safe_add(_, d), safe_add(f, i)), r), m);

        }



        function md5_ff(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {

            return md5_cmn(_ & m | ~_ & f, d, _, r, i, n);

        }



        function md5_gg(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {

            return md5_cmn(_ & f | m & ~f, d, _, r, i, n);

        }



        function md5_hh(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {

            return md5_cmn(_ ^ m ^ f, d, _, r, i, n);

        }



        function md5_ii(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {

            return md5_cmn(m ^ (_ | ~f), d, _, r, i, n);

        }



        function safe_add(d, _) {

            var m = (65535 & d) + (65535 & _);

            return (d >> 16) + (_ >> 16) + (m >> 16) << 16 | 65535 & m;

        }



        function bit_rol(d, _) {

            return d << _ | d >>> 32 - _;

        }



        function hashSha256(ascii) {

            function rightRotate(value, amount) {

                return (value >>> amount) | (value << (32 - amount));

            }



            var mathPow = Math.pow;

            var maxWord = mathPow(2, 32);

            var lengthProperty = 'length';

            var i, j; // Used as a counter across the whole file

            var result = '';



            var words = [];

            var asciiBitLength = ascii[lengthProperty] * 8;



            //* caching results is optional - remove/add slash from front of this line to toggle

            // Initial hash value: first 32 bits of the fractional parts of the square roots of the first 8 primes

            // (we actually calculate the first 64, but extra values are just ignored)

            var hash = hashSha256.h = hashSha256.h || [];

            // Round constants: first 32 bits of the fractional parts of the cube roots of the first 64 primes

            var k = hashSha256.k = hashSha256.k || [];

            var primeCounter = k[lengthProperty];

            /*/

            var hash = [], k = [];

            var primeCounter = 0;

            //*/



            var isComposite = {};

            for (var candidate = 2; primeCounter < 64; candidate++) {

                if (!isComposite[candidate]) {

                    for (i = 0; i < 313; i += candidate) {

                        isComposite[i] = candidate;

                    }

                    hash[primeCounter] = (mathPow(candidate, 0.5) * maxWord) | 0;

                    k[primeCounter++] = (mathPow(candidate, 1 / 3) * maxWord) | 0;

                }

            }



            ascii += '\x80'; // Append ' bit (plus zero padding)

            while (ascii[lengthProperty] % 64 - 56) ascii += '\x00';

            for (i = 0; i < ascii[lengthProperty]; i++) {

                j = ascii.charCodeAt(i);

                if (j >> 8) return; // ASCII check: only accept characters in range 0-255

                words[i >> 2] |= j << ((3 - i) % 4) * 8;

            }

            words[words[lengthProperty]] = ((asciiBitLength / maxWord) | 0);

            words[words[lengthProperty]] = (asciiBitLength);



            // process each chunk

            for (j = 0; j < words[lengthProperty];) {

                var w = words.slice(j, j += 16); // The message is expanded into 64 words as part of the iteration

                var oldHash = hash;

                // This is now the undefinedworking hash", often labelled as variables a...g

                // (we have to truncate as well, otherwise extra entries at the end accumulate

                hash = hash.slice(0, 8);



                for (i = 0; i < 64; i++) {

                    var i2 = i + j;

                    // Expand the message into 64 words

                    // Used below if 

                    var w15 = w[i - 15],

                        w2 = w[i - 2];



                    // Iterate

                    var a = hash[0],

                        e = hash[4];

                    var temp1 = hash[7] + (rightRotate(e, 6) ^ rightRotate(e, 11) ^ rightRotate(e, 25)) + ((e & hash[5]) ^ ((~e) & hash[6])) + k[i] + (w[i] = (i < 16) ? w[i] : (w[i - 16] + (rightRotate(w15, 7) ^ rightRotate(w15, 18) ^ (w15 >>> 3)) + w[i - 7] + (rightRotate(w2, 17) ^ rightRotate(w2, 19) ^ (w2 >>> 10))) | 0);

                    // This is only used once, so *could* be moved below, but it only saves 4 bytes and makes things unreadble

                    var temp2 = (rightRotate(a, 2) ^ rightRotate(a, 13) ^ rightRotate(a, 22)) + ((a & hash[1]) ^ (a & hash[2]) ^ (hash[1] & hash[2])); // maj



                    hash = [(temp1 + temp2) | 0].concat(hash); // We don't bother trimming off the extra ones, they're harmless as long as we're truncating when we do the slice()

                    hash[4] = (hash[4] + temp1) | 0;

                }



                for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {

                    hash[i] = (hash[i] + oldHash[i]) | 0;

                }

            }



            for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {

                for (j = 3; j + 1; j--) {

                    var b = (hash[i] >> (j * 8)) & 255;

                    result += ((b < 16) ? 0 : '') + b.toString(16);

                }

            }

            return result;

        }



        return {

            trackBehaviorInit: trackBehaviorInit,

            trackMonetate: trackMonetate,

            bindObjLoad: bindObjLoad,

            bindOn: bindOn,

            log: log,

            error: error,

            logList: logList,

            hashMd5: hashMd5,

            hashSha256: hashSha256,

            cookieDel: cookieDel,

            cookieGet: cookieGet,

            cookieSet: cookieSet

        };

    })();

});</script>

window.customAnalyticsCall = function(x) {



    var tempValue = "";

    var varValue = "";

    var tempEvents = "";

    var tempEvars = "";

    var tempProps = "";

    var tempLists = "";

    var tempLinkTrackVars = "";

    var tempLinkTrackEvents = "";



    s.origLTV = s.linkTrackVars;

    s.origLTE = s.linkTrackEvents;

    s.origEvents = s.events;

    s.linkTrackVars="";

    s.linkTrackEvents="";

    s.events="";



    /*check for events, evars, props*/

    if (typeof x != "undefined") {

        /*check capitalization of event, eVar, prop*/

        var regexE = /event/i;

        var regexV = /evar/i;

        var regexP = /prop/i;

        var regexL = /list/i;

        tempEvents = x.split("^");

        tempEvents.forEach(function(value, index) {

            /*test which variable type*/

            var varType = "";

            if (/^event/i.test(value) == true) {

                varType = "event";

            } else if (/^evar/i.test(value) == true) {

                varType = "eVar";

            } else if (/^prop/i.test(value) == true) {

                varType = "prop";

            } else if (/^list/i.test(value) == true) {

                varType = "list";

            }

            switch (varType) {

                case "event":

                    var eventVal = value.replace(regexE, "event");

                    s.events = s.apl(s.events, eventVal, ",", 2);

                    /*grab only the event name in case there is an incrementor also passed*/

                    var eventName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");

                    tempLinkTrackEvents = s.apl(tempLinkTrackEvents, eventName[0], ",", 2);

                    break;

                case "eVar":

                    /*split the evar and value*/

                    var varName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");

                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, varName[0].replace(regexV, "eVar"), ",", 2);

                    s[varName[0].replace(regexV, "eVar")] = varName[1];

                    break;

                case "prop":

                    /*split the prop and value*/

                    var propName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");

                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, propName[0].replace(regexP, "prop"), ",", 2);

                    s[propName[0].replace(regexP, "prop")] = propName[1];

                    break;

                case "list":

                    /*split the prop and value*/

                    var listName = value.replace("=", "@@").split("@@");

                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, listName[0].replace(regexL, "list"), ",", 2);

                    s[listName[0].replace(regexL, "list")] = listName[1].replace(/\^/g, "|").replace(/\;/g, ",");

                    break;

                default:

                    // add nothing

            }

        });

    }

    s.linkTrackEvents = tempLinkTrackEvents;

    s.linkTrackVars = tempLinkTrackVars;

    s.tl(this, "o", "Custom Analytics Call");

    s.events = s.origEvents;

    s.linkTrackVars = s.origLTV;

    s.linkTrackEvents = s.origLTE;

}

                if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.latitude=") > -1) {

                    var latitude = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.latitude=", '');

                }

                if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.stateProvince=") > -1) {

                    var stateProvince = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.stateProvince=", '');

                }

                if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.country=") > -1) {

                    var country = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.country=", '');

                }

                if (qsArr[i].indexOf("searchRadius=") > -1) {

                    var searchRadius = qsArr[i].replace("searchRadius=", '');

                }

            }

        }

        var type = "";

        if (propertyCode != '') {

            type = 'property';

        } else if (propertyCode == '' && stateProvince != '' && country != '') {

            type = 'state';

        } else if (propertyCode == '' && stateProvince == '' && country != '') {

            type = 'country';

        } else {

            type = 'destination';

        }

        //Getting Timestamp

        var dateNow = new Date();

        var timestampNow = dateNow.toISOString();

        var endOfRecord = "";

        if (!noCrrntSrch) {

            endOfRecord = ",";

        }

        var most_recent_search = '{ "displayName":"' + displayName + '" , "propertyCode":"' + propertyCode + '" , "longitude":"' + longitude + '" , "latitude":"' + latitude + '", "stateProvince":"' + stateProvince + '" , "country":"' + country + '" , "searchRadius":"' + searchRadius + '" , "timestamp":"' + timestampNow + '", "type":"' + type + '" }' + endOfRecord;

        if (current_searches_length == 5) {

            var last = current_recent_searches.lastIndexOf(",{");

            var tmpValue = current_recent_searches.slice(last, current_recent_searches.length);

            current_recent_searches = current_recent_searches.replace(tmpValue, '');

        }

        current_recent_searches = most_recent_search + current_recent_searches;

        localStorage.setItem("recent_searches", current_recent_searches);

    }

}

}

		});

	});

	function isEmpty(val) {

		return (val === undefined || val == null || val.length <= 0) ? true : false;

	}

	function key(obj) {

		return Object.keys(obj)

		.map(function (k) {

			return k + "" + obj[k];

		})

		.join("");

	}

	function distinct(arr) {

		var result = arr.reduce(function (acc, e) {

			acc[key(e)] = e;

			return acc;

		}, {});

		return Object.keys(result).map(function (k) {

			return result[k];

		});

	}



});</script>

function setCookie(name,value,days,theDomain) {

    var expires = "";

    if (days) {

        var date = new Date();

        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));

        expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();

    }

    document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; path=/; domain="+theDomain;

}



function deleteCookie(name) { setCookie(name, '', -1); }



});</script>

function setCookie(name, value, days) {

	let expires = '';

	if (days) {

		const date = new Date();

		date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));

		expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();

	}

	document.cookie = name + '=' + (value || '') + expires + ';' + 'path=/;';

}
